msg:After carefully selecting for a long time, I booked this homestay. Generally speaking, it is very unique among homestays. At the entrance of Chengkan Village, there is a special passage to the hotel. Along the Yongxing Lake, the pavilions, teahouses and guest rooms are presented one by one, which is amazing. The Guanhe King Bed Room we booked is at the innermost of the way, close to the exit door. Sitting in the room, you can listen to the sound of rain, watch the ripples of the lake, the white walls and black tiles, and the green mountains and clouds. It is beautiful. The staff is also very considerate. They helped us carry the boxes throughout the check-in and check-out process to avoid damaging the wheels on the bluestone road. The breakfast is also very rich. The topping noodles look very light, but the taste is really delicious.
However, I still want to talk about the room facilities. First of all, there is no window in the room. Maybe it‚Äôs because the first floor is facing the lake, but it does feel a bit stuffy when the door is closed at night. The room was renovated last year. There is a smell as soon as you enter the door. It is said to be the smell of the original color of wood, but it is still a bit heavy, especially after closing the door at night. In addition, the door had a problem and could not be locked. The staff came to fix the door at 10:30 pm. They were very nice and fixed it, but it still showed that the daily maintenance and inspection were not enough. In addition, the panel of the smart control Xiao Qiao cannot be completely dark at night, and the control panel indications of the two mirrors on the washbasin cannot be completely dark. The three panels make the room quite bright. I can't accept the light environment the most when I sleep. I cover the two panels with two pillows, and the other one is always shining. It may be the influence of light and smell. I woke up at five in the morning. I wanted to sleep until I woke up naturally, but I couldn't realize it.
I hope the facilities can be improved. I stayed in Xidi Bo Xin Yunshe these two days. It is also in the scenic area. It has a huge garden. More importantly, the room facilities are very attentive and of high quality, and the cost performance is much higher.

name:A‚Äçn‚Äço‚Äçn‚Äçy‚Äçm‚Äço‚Äçu‚Äçs‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Lotus View Twin Room
info:Stayed in March 2024

info:9 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted March 2, 2024
msg:Visit Chengkan, and you will have no troubles in your life.
Chengkan was originally named Longxi. It was built in the Eastern Han Dynasty and the Three Kingdoms period more than 1,800 years ago. The whole village is arranged according to the Eight Diagrams of the Book of Changes, "Yin (Kan), Yang (Cheng), two qi unify the unity of heaven and man", and the three streets and ninety-nine lanes are like a maze. The ancient Longxi River in the village is like a jade belt, passing through the village in an S shape to form the dividing line of the Eight Diagrams Yin and Yang fish. The eight mountains around the village naturally form the eight directions of the Eight Diagrams, forming a natural Eight Diagrams layout.
This trip gave up staying in Banyan Tree and chose Shudetang. The 38th generation of Su Che's descendants let this 900-year-old old house give it a new word and become a place for more people to stay.
It is said that Carina Lau will stay here every time she comes to Huangshan. It is really the ceiling of Hui-style hotels. The housekeeper added VX in advance and waited for the entrance of the scenic spot to greet me early. The service at the check-in time was really super super considerate, and he also helped to make an appoin**ent for the scenic spot explanation according to my request.
The hotel area is quite large, with its own lake, a total of more than a dozen rooms, and you can also choose to eat outdoors. You must make reservations in advance during the peak season (given that I was traveling on a whim, I was lucky to be able to make reservations~)
From the perspective of the old house, whether it is sunny or rainy, early in the morning or at dusk, whether it is by the lotus pond, under the big tree or in front of the window, there is always a Huizhou ink painting in front of you. Watch the willows in spring, the lotus in summer, the fields in autumn, and the snow in winter~
